2024-06-11 22:22:02,166 - root - INFO - |A : The concept behind real-time indexing in LlamaIndex.io involves ingesting, structuring, and providing access to private or domain-specific data for LLM-based applications. It uses data connectors to bring in data, data indexes to organize it, and engines for natural language access. The system follows a Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) approach, where it retrieves information, includes it in the question for context, and prompts the LLM to generate an answer based on the enriched prompt. This approach is cost-effective, up-to-date, and reliable for data augmentation, addressing the limitations of fine-tuning LLMs. LlamaIndex.io caters to both novice and advanced users, offering a high-level API for easy use and lower-level APIs for customization.
